     1 import { useEffect } from 'react';
     2 import { useNavigate, useLocation } from 'react-router-dom';
     3 import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
     4 import { toast } from 'sonner';
     5 
     6 interface RouteGuardProps {
     7   children: React.ReactNode;
     8 }
     9 
    10 // Please add the pages that can be accessed without logging in to PUBLIC_ROUTES.
    11 const PUBLIC_ROUTES = [
    12   '/',
    13   '/login',
    14   '/signup',
    15   '/admin-setup',
    16   '/verify-email',
    17   '/reset-password',
    18   '/forgot-password',
    19   '/terms-and-conditions',
    20   '/privacy-policy',
    21   '/contact',
    22   '/events',
    23   '/403',
    24   '/404'
    25 ];
    26 
    27 function matchPublicRoute(path: string, patterns: string[]) {
    28   return patterns.some(pattern => {
    29     if (pattern.includes('*')) {
    30       const regex = new RegExp('^' + pattern.replace('*', '.*') + '$');
    31       return regex.test(path);
    32     }
    33     return path === pattern;
    34   });
    35 }
    36 
    37 export function RouteGuard({ children }: RouteGuardProps) {
    38   const { user, profile, loading } = useAuth();
    39   const navigate = useNavigate();
    40   const location = useLocation();
    41 
    42   useEffect(() => {
    43     if (loading) return;
    44 
    45     const isPublic = matchPublicRoute(location.pathname, PUBLIC_ROUTES);
    46 
    47     if (!user && !isPublic) {
    48       navigate('/login', { state: { from: location.pathname }, replace: true });
    49       return;
    50     }
    51 
    52     // Admin Route Protection
    53     const isAdminRoute = location.pathname === '/admin' || location.pathname.startsWith('/admin/');
    54     const isUserAdmin = profile?.role === 'admin' || profile?.role === 'super_admin';
    55     
    56     if (isAdminRoute && !isUserAdmin) {
    57       toast.error('Unauthorized access. Admin privileges required.');
    58       navigate('/', { replace: true });
    59     }
    60   }, [user, profile, loading, location.pathname, navigate]);
    61 
    62   if (loading) {
    63     return (
    64       <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen">
    65         <div className="animate-spin rounded-full h-12 w-12 border-b-2 border-primary"></div>
    66       </div>
    67     );
    68   }
    69 
    70   return <>{children}</>;
    71 }

</observation>

    76     }
    77     if (password.length < 6) {
    78       toast.error('Password must be at least 6 characters');
    79       return;
    80     }
    81 
    82     setLoading(true);
    83     try {
    84       const { data, error } = await invokeEdgeFunction('reset-password-otp', {
    85         body: { email, otp, new_password: password }
    86       });
    87 
    88       if (error) throw error;
    89 
    90       toast.success(data?.message || 'Password reset successful! You can now login with your new password.');
    91       setStep('email');
    92       setEmail('');
    93       setOtp('');
    94       setPassword('');
    95       setConfirmPassword('');
    96     } catch (error: any) {
    97       toast.error(error.message || 'Failed to reset password');
    98       console.error(error);
    99     } finally {
   100       setLoading(false);
   101     }
   102   };

    48 export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
    49   const [user, setUser] = React.useState<User | null>(null);
    50   const [profile, setProfile] = React.useState<Profile | null>(null);
    51   const [loading, setLoading] = React.useState(true);
    52   const { trackSignIn, trackSignUp } = useAnalytics();
    53 
    54   const refreshProfile = async () => {
    55     if (!user) {
    56       setProfile(null);
    57       return;
    58     }
    59 
    60     const profileData = await getProfile(user.id);
    61     setProfile(profileData);
    62   };

    64   React.useEffect(() => {
    65     supabase
    66       .auth
    67       .getSession()
    68       .then(async ({ data: { session } }) => {
    69         setUser(session?.user ?? null);
    70         if (session?.user) {
    71           const profileData = await getProfile(session.user.id);
    72           setProfile(profileData);
    73         }
    74       })
    75       .catch(error => {
    76         // @ts-ignore

    78       })

    80         setLoading(false);
    81       });

    83     // In this function, do NOT use any await calls. Use `.then()` instead to avoid deadlocks.
    84     const { data: { subscription } } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange((event, session) => {
    85       setUser(session?.user ?? null);
    86       
    87       if (event === 'SIGNED_IN' && session?.user) {

    91 
    92       if (session?.user) {
    93         // Use a small delay to ensure trigger has finished and profile is visible

    95           getProfile(session.user.id).then((p) => {

    97               setProfile(p);
    98               
    99               const isUserAdmin = p.role === 'admin' || p.role === 'super_admin';
   100               if (isUserAdmin) {
   101                 // Admin specific logic if needed
   102               }

   104               // Handle referral if user is new and was just created
   105               const ref = sessionStorage.getItem('referral_code');
   106               if (!p.referrer_id && ref) {
   107                 const userCreated = new Date(session.user.created_at).getTime();
   108                 const now = new Date().getTime();
   109                 // If user was created in the last 2 minutes, try to attribute referral
   110                 if (now - userCreated < 120000) {
   111                   supabase.from('profiles').select('id').eq('referral_code', ref).maybeSingle().then(({ data: referrer }) => {

   113                       (supabase.from('profiles') as any).update({ referrer_id: (referrer as any).id }).eq('id', session.user.id).then(() => {
   114                         console.log('Referral attributed successfully');
   115                         sessionStorage.removeItem('referral_code');
   116                         refreshProfile();
   117                       });
   118                     }
   119                   });
   120                 }
   121               }
   122             } else if (retryCount < 3) {
   123               // Retry fetching profile if not found yet (replication/trigger lag)
   124               setTimeout(() => checkReferral(retryCount + 1), 1000);
   125             }
   126           });
   127         };
   128         
   129         checkReferral();
   130       } else {
   131         setProfile(null);
   132       }
   133     });
   134

   138   const signInWithEmail = async (email: string, password: string) => {
   139     try {

   141         .from('profiles') as any)

   157             ip_address: 'browser_client',

   165           throw new Error('Email login is not currently enabled for this platform. Please contact support.');
   166         }
   167         throw error;
   168       }
   169 
   170       if (isUserAdmin && authData.user) {
   171         await (supabase.from('admin_security_logs') as any).insert({

   183       return { error: error as Error };

   187   const signUpWithEmail = async (

   194       // Use provided code or check session storage

   222       });
   223 
   224       if (error) {
   225         if (error.message.includes('provider is not enabled') || error.message.includes('Unsupported provider')) {
   226           throw new Error('Email registration is not currently enabled for this platform. Please contact support.');
   227         }
   228         throw error;
   229       }
   230 
   231       // Update profile with additional data if user was created
   232       // This is now redundant as handle_new_user trigger handles metadata, 
   233       // but we keep it as a fallback, ensuring it doesn't block the return.
   234       if (data.user && additionalData) {
   235         trackSignUp('email');
   236         supabase
   237           .from('profiles')
   238           // @ts-ignore - Supabase type inference issue
   239           .update({
   240             full_name: additionalData.full_name,
   241             phone: additionalData.phone,
   242             country: additionalData.country
   243           })

   245           .then(({ error: updateError }) => {
   246             if (updateError) console.warn('Secondary profile update failed (likely RLS), but user was created:', updateError);
   247           });
   248       }
   249 
   250       return { error: null };
   251     } catch (error) {
   252       return { error: error as Error };
   253     }
   254   };
   255 
   256   const signInWithGoogle = async () => {
   257     try {
   258       const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithOAuth({
   259         provider: 'google',
   260         options: {
   261           redirectTo: window.location.origin,
   262         },
   263       });
   264 
   265       if (error) {
   266         // Provide more helpful error for disabled providers

   281   const verifyOTP = async (email: string, token: string, purpose: 'signup' | 'login' | 'password_reset' | 'admin_login' = 'signup') => {
   282     try {
   283       const { data, error } = await invokeEdgeFunction('verify-otp', {
   284         body: { email, otp: token, purpose }
   285       });
   286 
   287       if (error) throw error;
   288       
   289       if (data?.redirect_url) {
   290         // For admin OTP login, we get a magic link back

   292         return { error: null };

   294 
   295       if (data?.user) {

   304   const resendOTP = async (email: string, purpose: 'signup' | 'login' | 'password_reset' | 'admin_login' = 'signup', userData?: any) => {
   305     try {
   306       const { error } = await invokeEdgeFunction('send-otp', {
   307         body: { email, purpose, userData }
   308       });
   309 
   310       if (error) throw error;
   311       return { error: null };
   312     } catch (error) {
   313       return { error: error as Error };
   314     }
   315   };
   316 
   317   const resetPassword = async (email: string) => {
   318     try {
   319       const { error } = await supabase.auth.resetPasswordForEmail(email, {
   320         redirectTo: `${window.location.origin}/reset-password`
   321       });
   322 
   323       if (error) throw error;
   324       return { error: null };
   325     } catch (error) {
   326       return { error: error as Error };
   327     }
   328   };
   329 
   330    const signOut = async () => {
   331     await supabase.auth.signOut();
   332     setUser(null);
   333     setProfile(null);
   334   };
   335 
   336   const isAdmin = profile?.role === 'admin' || profile?.role === 'super_admin';
   337   const isSuperAdmin = profile?.role === 'super_admin';
   338 
   339   return (
   340     <AuthContext.Provider value={{ 
   341       user, profile, isAdmin, isSuperAdmin, loading,
   342       signInWithEmail, signUpWithEmail, signInWithGoogle, verifyOTP, resendOTP, 
   343       resetPassword, signOut, refreshProfile
   344     }}>
   345       {children}
   346     </AuthContext.Provider>
   347   );
   348 }
   349 
   350 export function useAuth() {
   351   const context = React.useContext(AuthContext);
   352   if (context === undefined) {
   353     throw new Error('useAuth must be used within an AuthProvider');
   354   }
   355   return context;
   356 }

     8 
     9 /**
    10  * Robust wrapper for invoking Supabase Edge Functions.
    11  * Automatically parses error context and returns a user-friendly error message.
    12  */
    13 export async function invokeEdgeFunction<T = any>(
    14   name: string,
    15   options?: FunctionInvokeOptions
    16 ): Promise<{ data: T | null; error: Error | null }> {
    17   try {
    18     const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke(name, {
    19       body: options?.body,
    20       headers: options?.headers,
    21       method: options?.method,
    22     });
    23 
    24     if (error) {
    25       let errorMsg = error.message;
    26       try {
    27         if (error.context && typeof error.context.text === 'function') {
    28           const contextText = await error.context.text();
    29           try {
    30             const contextJson = JSON.parse(contextText);
    31             errorMsg = contextJson.error || contextJson.message || contextText;
    32           } catch (e) {
    33             errorMsg = contextText;
    34           }
    35         } else if (error.context && typeof error.context === 'string') {
    36           errorMsg = error.context;
    37         }
    38       } catch (e) {
    39         console.error(`Error parsing ${name} error context:`, e);
    40       }
    41       
    42       // If it's the generic Supabase error message, try to make it better
    43       if (errorMsg === 'Edge Function returned a non-2xx status code') {
    44         errorMsg = `Server error in ${name}. Please try again later.`;
    45       }
    46       
    47       return { data: null, error: new Error(errorMsg) };
    48     }
    49 
    50     return { data: data as T, error: null };
    51   } catch (error: any) {
    52     console.error(`Unexpected exception invoking ${name}:`, error);
    53     return { data: null, error: error as Error };
    54   }
    55 }

</observation>

```
import { Bell, Check, Info, AlertTriangle, X } from 'lucide-react';
import {
  Sheet,
  SheetContent,
  SheetHeader,
  SheetTitle,
  SheetTrigger,
} from '@/components/ui/sheet';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { ScrollArea } from '@/components/ui/scroll-area';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { useState } from 'react';

interface Notification {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
  time: string;
  type: 'info' | 'success' | 'warning' | 'error';
  unread: boolean;
}

export function RightSlider() {
  const [notifications, setNotifications] = useState<Notification[]>([
    {
      id: '1',
      title: 'Deposit Successful',
      description: 'Your deposit of 500 USDT has been confirmed.',
      time: '2 mins ago',
      type: 'success',
      unread: true,
    },
    {
      id: '2',
      title: 'New Referral',
      description: 'A new user joined using your referral link.',
      time: '1 hour ago',
      type: 'info',
      unread: true,
    },
    {
      id: '3',
      title: 'Security Alert',
      description: 'New login detected from a new IP address.',
      time: '3 hours ago',
      type: 'warning',
      unread: false,
    },
    {
      id: '4',
      title: 'Market Update',
      description: 'Gold prices are up by 1.5% today.',
      time: '5 hours ago',
      type: 'info',
      unread: false,
    },
  ]);

  const markAllRead = () => {
    setNotifications(prev => prev.map(n => ({ ...n, unread: false })));
  };

  const removeNotification = (id: string) => {
    setNotifications(prev => prev.filter(n => n.id !== id));
  };

  const unreadCount = notifications.filter(n => n.unread).length;

  return (
    <Sheet>
      <SheetTrigger asChild>
        <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="relative group">
          <Bell className="h-5 w-5 text-muted-foreground group-hover:text-primary transition-colors" />
          {unreadCount > 0 && (
            <span className="absolute top-1.5 right-1.5 flex h-2 w-2">
              <span className="animate-ping absolute inline-flex h-full w-full rounded-full bg-primary opacity-75"></span>
              <span className="relative inline-flex rounded-full h-2 w-2 bg-primary"></span>
            </span>
          )}
        </Button>
      </SheetTrigger>
      <SheetContent side="right" className="w-full sm:max-w-md p-0 flex flex-col v56-glass border-l border-white/10">
        <SheetHeader className="p-6 border-b border-white/10">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <SheetTitle className="text-xl font-black v56-gradient-text">Notifications</SheetTitle>
            {unreadCount > 0 && (
              <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={markAllRead} className="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold tracking-widest text-primary hover:bg-primary/10">
                Mark all read
              </Button>
            )}
          </div>
        </SheetHeader>

        <ScrollArea className="flex-1">
          <div className="p-4 space-y-4">
            {notifications.length > 0 ? (
              notifications.map((notification) => (
                <div
                  key={notification.id}
                  className={cn(
                    "p-4 rounded-2xl border transition-all duration-300 relative group",
                    notification.unread 
                      ? "bg-primary/5 border-primary/20" 
                      : "bg-white/5 border-white/5 opacity-70 hover:opacity-100"
                  )}
                >
                  <div className="flex gap-4">
                    <div className={cn(
                      "mt-1 p-2 rounded-xl shrink-0",
                      notification.type === 'success' && "bg-green-500/10 text-green-500",
                      notification.type === 'info' && "bg-blue-500/10 text-blue-500",
                      notification.type === 'warning' && "bg-yellow-500/10 text-yellow-500",
                      notification.type === 'error' && "bg-red-500/10 text-red-500",
                    )}>
                      {notification.type === 'success' && <Check className="h-4 w-4" />}
                      {notification.type === 'info' && <Info className="h-4 w-4" />}
                      {notification.type === 'warning' && <AlertTriangle className="h-4 w-4" />}
                      {notification.type === 'error' && <AlertTriangle className="h-4 w-4" />}
                    </div>
                    
                    <div className="flex-1 space-y-1">
                      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                        <h4 className="text-sm font-bold uppercase tracking-tight">{notification.title}</h4>
                        <span className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground font-medium uppercase tracking-widest">{notification.time}</span>
                      </div>
                      <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed">
                        {notification.description}
                      </p>
                    </div>

                    <Button 
                      variant="ghost" 
                      size="icon" 
                      className="h-6 w-6 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity"
                      onClick={() => removeNotification(notification.id)}
                    >
                      <X className="h-3 w-3" />
                    </Button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))
            ) : (
              <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center py-20 text-center space-y-4">
                <div className="p-4 rounded-full bg-muted/50">
                  <Bell className="h-8 w-8 text-muted-foreground opacity-20" />
                </div>
                <div className="space-y-1">
                  <p className="font-bold text-sm uppercase tracking-widest">No notifications</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">You're all caught up!</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </ScrollArea>

        <div className="p-6 border-t border-white/10 bg-black/20">
          <Button className="w-full font-bold uppercase tracking-widest text-xs h-12 rounded-xl group" variant="outline">
            View All Activity
            <Bell className="ml-2 h-4 w-4 group-hover:animate-bounce" />
          </Button>
        </div>
      </SheetContent>
    </Sheet>
  );
}

function cn(...inputs: any[]) {
  return inputs.filter(Boolean).join(' ');
}
```

```
              <Bell className={cn('w-5 h-5 transition-transform group-hover:scale-110')} />
              {unreadCount > 0 && (
                <span className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 flex h-2 w-2">
                  <span className="relative inline-flex rounded-full h-2 w-2 bg-primary"></span>
                </span>
              )}
            </div>
            {!isCollapsed && <span className="text-sm font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">Activity Log</span>}
            {isCollapsed && (
              <div className="absolute left-full ml-4 px-3 py-1 bg-popover text-popover-foreground rounded-md text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-widest opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity whitespace-nowrap z-50 pointer-events-none border border-border shadow-xl">
                Activity Log
              </div>
            )}
          </button>
        ) : (
          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="relative group hover:bg-primary/10 hover:text-primary transition-all hidden md:flex">
            <Bell className="h-5 w-5 text-muted-foreground group-hover:text-primary transition-colors" />
            {unreadCount > 0 && (
              <span className="absolute top-2 right-2 flex h-2 w-2">
                <span className="animate-ping absolute inline-flex h-full w-full rounded-full bg-primary opacity-75"></span>
                <span className="relative inline-flex rounded-full h-2 w-2 bg-primary border border-background"></span>
              </span>
            )}
          </Button>
        )}
      </SheetTrigger>

```

</action>

# User Requirement
Please design a user interface (UI) feature for a website or application based on the following requirement.

1.  **Core Objective:** Implement a dedicated, separate scrollbar for a navigation area (nav) within the interface.

2.  **Detailed Requirements:**
    *   The scrollbar must be visually distinct from any main content or global scrollbar.
    *   It should control scrolling *only* within the boundaries of the navigation panel.
    *   The navigation content should become scrollable only when its content height exceeds the available vertical space of the nav container.

3.  **Functional Specifications:**
    *   **Trigger:** The separate scrollbar must appear automatically when the navigation content overflows its container.
    *   **Behavior:** The scrollbar must allow smooth vertical scrolling of the navigation items.
    *   **Scope:** Scrolling via this nav scrollbar must not affect the position of any other page elements or the main window's scroll position.

4.  **Design & Usability Considerations:**
    *   **Visibility:** The scrollbar should be clearly visible and accessible to users.
    *   **Styling:** Provide suggestions for styling (e.g., color, width, hover effects) to ensure it matches the overall design theme while remaining functionally clear.
    *   **Platform Consistency:** Consider operating system conventions (e.g., overlay scrollbars on macOS vs. persistent scrollbars on Windows) if relevant.

Please provide a technical implementation approach (e.g., using CSS `overflow` properties) along with a brief visual mockup or description of the styled component.

     1 import { supabase } from '@/db/supabase';
     2 
     3 // Convert base64 string to Uint8Array for VAPID key
     4 function urlBase64ToUint8Array(base64String: string) {
     5   const padding = '='.repeat((4 - (base64String.length % 4)) % 4);
     6   const base64 = (base64String + padding).replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/');
     7   const rawData = window.atob(base64);
     8   const outputArray = new Uint8Array(rawData.length);
     9   for (let i = 0; i < rawData.length; ++i) {
    10     outputArray[i] = rawData.charCodeAt(i);
    11   }
    12   return outputArray;
    13 }
    14 
    15 export async function subscribeToPush(userId: string) {
    16   if (!('serviceWorker' in navigator) || !('PushManager' in window)) {
    17     throw new Error('Push notifications are not supported in this browser');
    18   }
    19 
    20   const registration = await navigator.serviceWorker.ready;
    21 
    22   // Get VAPID public key from settings or a known place
    23   // For simplicity, we assume it's available in an env var or we fetch it
    24   const { data: settings } = await supabase
    25     .from('settings')
    26     .select('*')
    27     .in('key', ['vapid_public_key', 'vapid_subject']) as { data: any[] | null };
    28 
    29   const publicVapidKey = settings?.find((s: any) => s.key === 'vapid_public_key')?.value || import.meta.env.VITE_VAPID_PUBLIC_KEY;
    30   // const vapidSubject = settings?.find((s: any) => s.key === 'vapid_subject')?.value || 'mailto:info@goldxusdt.com';
    31 
    32   if (!publicVapidKey) {
    33     throw new Error('VAPID public key not found');
    34   }
    35 
    36   const subscription = await registration.pushManager.subscribe({
    37     userVisibleOnly: true,
    38     applicationServerKey: urlBase64ToUint8Array(publicVapidKey)
    39   });
    40 
    41   // Save subscription to database
    42   const { error } = await supabase.from('push_subscriptions').upsert({
    43     user_id: userId,
    44     subscription_json: subscription.toJSON(),
    45     updated_at: new Date().toISOString()
    46   } as any, { onConflict: 'user_id' });
    47 
    48   if (error) throw error;
    49 
    50   return subscription;
    51 }
    52 
    53 export async function unsubscribeFromPush(userId: string) {
    54   if (!('serviceWorker' in navigator)) return;
    55 
    56   const registration = await navigator.serviceWorker.ready;
    57   const subscription = await registration.pushManager.getSubscription();
    58 
    59   if (subscription) {
    60     await subscription.unsubscribe();
    61   }
    62 
    63   const { error } = await supabase
    64     .from('push_subscriptions')
    65     .delete()
    66     .eq('user_id', userId);
    67 
    68   if (error) throw error;
    69 }
    70 
    71 export async function getSubscriptionData(userId: string) {
    72   const { data, error } = await supabase
    73     .from('push_subscriptions')
    74     .select('*')
    75     .eq('user_id', userId)
    76     .maybeSingle();
    77 
    78   if (error) throw error;
    79   return data;
    80 }
    81 
    82 export async function updateSubscriptionPreferences(userId: string, categories: string[]) {
    83   const { error } = await supabase
    84     .from('push_subscriptions')
    85     // @ts-ignore
    86     .update({ categories })
    87     .eq('user_id', userId);
    88 
    89   if (error) throw error;
    90 }
    91 
    92 export async function getSubscriptionStatus(userId: string) {
    93   const data = await getSubscriptionData(userId);
    94   return !!data;
    95 }
    96 
    97 export function registerServiceWorker() {
    98   if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
    99     window.addEventListener('load', () => {
   100       navigator.serviceWorker.register('/sw.js').then(
   101         (registration) => {
   102           console.log('ServiceWorker registration successful with scope: ', registration.scope);
   103         },
   104         (err) => {
   105           console.log('ServiceWorker registration failed: ', err);
   106         }
   107       );
   108     });
   109   }

    70 export default function AdvancedReferralPage() {
    71   const { user } = useAuth();
    72   const navigate = useNavigate();
    73   const [downline, setDownline] = useState<DownlineUser[]>([]);
    74   const [stats, setStats] = useState<CommissionStat[]>([]);
    75   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    76   const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState('');
    77   const [levelFilter, setLevelFilter] = useState('all');
    78   const [expandedNodes, setExpandedNodes] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set());
    79 
    80   useEffect(() => {
    81     if (user) {
    82       loadData();
    83     }
    84   }, [user]);
    85 
    86   const loadData = async () => {
    87     if (!user) return;
    88     setLoading(true);
    89     try {
    90       const { data: downlineData, error: downlineError } = await (supabase.rpc as any)('get_downline_network', { 
    91         p_user_id: user.id 
    92       });
    93 
    94       if (downlineError) throw downlineError;
    95 
    96       const { data: statsData, error: statsError } = await (supabase.rpc as any)('get_referral_commission_stats', { 
    97         p_user_id: user.id 
    98       });
    99 
   100       if (statsError) throw statsError;
   101 
   102       setDownline(downlineData || []);
   103       setStats(statsData || []);
   104     } catch (error) {
   105       console.error('Failed to load referral data:', error);
   106       toast.error('Failed to load referral data');
   107     } finally {
   108       setLoading(false);
   109     }
   110   };
   111 
   112   const toggleNode = (userId: string) => {
   113     const newExpanded = new Set(expandedNodes);
   114     if (newExpanded.has(userId)) {
   115       newExpanded.delete(userId);
   116     } else {
   117       newExpanded.add(userId);
   118     }
   119     setExpandedNodes(newExpanded);
   120   };
   121 
   122   const buildTree = (users: DownlineUser[]) => {
   123     const userMap = new Map<string, DownlineUser>();
   124     const rootNodes: DownlineUser[] = [];
   125 
   126     // Initialize all nodes
   127     users.forEach(u => {
   128       userMap.set(u.user_id, { ...u, children: [] });
   129     });
   130 
   131     // Link nodes to their parents
   132     users.forEach(u => {
   133       const node = userMap.get(u.user_id)!;
   134       if (u.referrer_id === user?.id) {
   135         rootNodes.push(node);
   136       } else {
   137         const parent = userMap.get(u.referrer_id);
   138         if (parent) {
   139           parent.children?.push(node);
   140         }
   141       }
   142     });
   143 
   144     return rootNodes;
   145   };
   146 
   147   const filteredDownline = downline.filter(u => {

   150     const matchesLevel = levelFilter === 'all' || u.level === parseInt(levelFilter);

     1 CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION get_downline_network(p_user_id UUID, p_max_levels INTEGER DEFAULT 15)
     2 RETURNS TABLE (
     3   user_id UUID,
     4   username TEXT,
     5   email TEXT,
     6   level INTEGER,
     7   referrer_id UUID,
     8   created_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
     9   kyc_status public.kyc_status,
    10   is_active BOOLEAN
    11 ) AS $$
    12 BEGIN
    13   RETURN QUERY
    14   WITH RECURSIVE downline AS (
    15     -- Initial base case (direct referrals)
    16     SELECT 
    17       p.id as user_id, 
    18       p.username, 
    19       p.email, 
    20       1 as level, 
    21       p.referrer_id, 
    22       p.created_at, 
    23       p.kyc_status, 
    24       p.is_active
    25     FROM profiles p
    26     WHERE p.referrer_id = p_user_id
    27     
    28     UNION ALL
    29     
    30     -- Recursive step
    31     SELECT 
    32       p.id, 
    33       p.username, 
    34       p.email, 
    35       d.level + 1, 
    36       p.referrer_id, 
    37       p.created_at, 
    38       p.kyc_status, 
    39       p.is_active
    40     FROM profiles p
    41     INNER JOIN downline d ON p.referrer_id = d.user_id
    42     WHERE d.level < p_max_levels
    43   )
    44   SELECT * FROM downline;
    45 END;
    46 $$ LANGUAGE plpgsql SECURITY DEFINER;
    47 
    48 CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION get_referral_commission_stats(p_user_id UUID)
    49 RETURNS TABLE (
    50   level INTEGER,
    51   total_commission DECIMAL(20, 8),
    52   member_count INTEGER,
    53   commission_rate DECIMAL(20, 8)
    54 ) AS $$
    55 BEGIN
    56   RETURN QUERY
    57   WITH RECURSIVE downline AS (
    58     -- Initial base case
    59     SELECT p.id, 1 as level
    60     FROM profiles p
    61     WHERE p.referrer_id = p_user_id
    62     
    63     UNION ALL
    64     
    65     -- Recursive step
    66     SELECT p.id, d.level + 1
    67     FROM profiles p
    68     INNER JOIN downline d ON p.referrer_id = d.user_id
    69     WHERE d.level < 15
    70   ),
    71   stats AS (
    72     SELECT 
    73       d.level,
    74       COALESCE(SUM(rc.commission_amount), 0) as total_commission,
    75       COUNT(DISTINCT d.id) as member_count
    76     FROM downline d
    77     LEFT JOIN referral_commissions rc ON rc.referred_user_id = d.id AND rc.referrer_id = p_user_id AND rc.level = d.level
    78     GROUP BY d.level
    79   )
    80   SELECT 
    81     s.level,
    82     s.total_commission,
    83     s.member_count,
    84     (SELECT (COALESCE(value, '0')::DECIMAL / 100.0)
    85      FROM settings 
    86      WHERE key = 'level' || s.level || '_commission'
    87         OR key = 'referral_level' || s.level || '_commission'
    88         OR key = 'referral_level' || s.level || '_percentage'
    89      ORDER BY (
    90        CASE 
    91          WHEN key = 'level' || s.level || '_commission' THEN 1
    92          WHEN key = 'referral_level' || s.level || '_commission' THEN 2
    93          ELSE 3
    94        END
    95      ) ASC
    96      LIMIT 1) as commission_rate
    97   FROM stats s
    98   ORDER BY s.level ASC;
    99 END;
   100 $$ LANGUAGE plpgsql SECURITY DEFINER;

```
function urlBase64ToUint8Array(base64String: string) {
  const padding = '='.repeat((4 - (base64String.length % 4)) % 4);
  const base64 = (base64String + padding).replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/');
  const rawData = window.atob(base64);
  const outputArray = new Uint8Array(rawData.length);
  for (let i = 0; i < rawData.length; ++i) {
    outputArray[i] = rawData.charCodeAt(i);
  }
  return outputArray;
}

```
New String: ```
function urlBase64ToUint8Array(base64String: string) {
  const padding = '='.repeat((4 - (base64String.length % 4)) % 4);
  const base64 = (base64String + padding).replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/');
  const rawData = window.atob(base64);
  const outputArray = new Uint8Array(rawData.length);
  for (let i = 0; i < rawData.length; ++i) {
    outputArray[i] = rawData.charCodeAt(i);
  }

  // If the key is in DER format (SubjectPublicKeyInfo), extract the raw 65-byte public key
  // Raw uncompressed P-256 public key starts with 0x04 and is 65 bytes long
  if (outputArray.length > 65) {
    return outputArray.slice(-65);
  }

  return outputArray;
}

```
